  2239. # [20:27] <bz> On return from the JSNative there are thus 4 states:
  2240. # [20:27] * chmanchester is now known as chmanchester|afk
  2241. # [20:28] <bz> 1) return true, throwing false: Everything is great, keep going.
  2242. # [20:28] * Joins: Boriss (Boriss@moz-f1bjd5.PUBLIC.monkeybrains.net)
  2243. # [20:28] <bz> 2) return true, throwing true: The JSNative fucked up and violated the API contract. Some hapless next bit of code will get fatal assertions.
  2244. # [20:29] <bz> 3) return false, throwing true: The JSNative threw an exception, which is now stored in cx->pendingException or something like that.
  2245. # [20:29] * Quits: aklotz (Thunderbird@moz-1jtcvi.cg.shawcable.net) (Client exited)

  2247. # [20:29] <@ehsan> right
  2248. # [20:29] <Ms2ger> 4) OOM
  2249. # [20:29] <bz> 4) return false, throwing false: The JSNative threw an uncatchable exception. Terminate the script.
  2250. # [20:30] <bz> OOM is catchable.
  2251. # [20:30] <bz> (yes, that's insane)
